[1;30r[27;9H[36m</div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<div [31mid=[32m"changes"[36m></div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HConfiguration Overview[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m</div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HUbuntu's Apache2 default configuration is different from the[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hupstream default configuration, and split into several files optimized$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hinteraction with Ubuntu tools. The configuration system is[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H(B[0;1m[35m<b>[39m(B[mfully documented in[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H/usr/share/doc/apache2/README.Debian.gz(B[0;1m[35m</b>[39m(B[m. Refer to this for the full[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hdocumentation. Documentation for the web server itself can be[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hfound by accessing the [36m<a [31mhref=[32m"/manual"[36m>[39m(B[mmanual[36m</a>[39m(B[m if the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mapache2$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hpackage was installed on this server.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m</p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HThe configuration layout for an Apache2 web server installation on Ubu$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m</p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<pre>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H/etc/apache2/[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|-- apache2.conf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|[9G`--  ports.conf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|-- mods-enabled[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|[9G|-- *.load[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|[9G`-- *.conf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|-- conf-enabled[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|[9G`-- *.conf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|-- sites-enabled[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;1H|[9G`-- *.conf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m</pre>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<ul>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m<li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[39m(B[mapache2.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m is the main configuration[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hfile. It puts the pieces together by including all remainin$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hfiles when starting up the web server.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m</li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m<li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[39m(B[mports.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m is always included from the[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hmain configuration file. It is used to determine the listen$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hincoming connections, and this file can be customized anyti$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m</li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m<li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28HConfiguration files in the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mmods-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[39m(B[mconf-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m and [36m<tt>[39m(B[msites-enabled/[36m</tt>[39m(B[m director$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hparticular configuration snippets which manage modules, glo$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hfragments, or virtual host configurations, respectively.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m</li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m<li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28HThey are activated by symlinking available[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hconfiguration files from their respective[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H*-available/ counterparts. These should be managed[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hby using our helpers[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2enmod,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2dismod,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m</tt>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2ensite,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2dissite,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;29H[36m</tt>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Hand[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m<tt>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2enconf,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;33Ha2disconf[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H[36m</tt>[39m(B[m. See their respective man pages for detailed informat$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m</li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m<li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28HThe binary is called apache2. Due to the use of[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Henvironment variables, in the default configuration, apache$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hstarted/stopped with [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/etc/init.d/apache2[36m</tt>[39m(B[m or [36m<tt>[39m(B[map$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28H(B[0;1m[35m<b>[39m(B[mCalling [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/usr/bin/apache2[36m</tt>[39m(B[m directly will not work$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;28Hdefault configuration.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;25H[36m</li>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m</ul>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m</div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;13H[36m<div [31mid=[32m"docroot"[36m></div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HDocument Roots[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m</div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"content_section_text"[36m>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;13H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HBy default, Ubuntu does not allow access through the web browser to[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H[36m<em>[39m(B[many[36m</em>[39m(B[m file apart of those located in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/var/www[36m</tt>[39m(B[m,[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H[36m<a [31mhref=[32m"http://httpd.apache.org/docs/2.4/mod/mod_userdir.html"[36m [31mrel=[32m"n[39m(B[m$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hdirectories (when enabled) and [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/usr/share[36m</tt>[39m(B[m (for web[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Happlications). If your site is using a web document root[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hlocated elsewhere (such as in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/srv[36m</tt>[39m(B[m) you may need to whitelist$[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hdocument root directory in [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/etc/apache2/apache2.conf[36m</tt>[39m(B[m.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;13H[36m</p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;13H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HThe default Ubuntu document root is [36m<tt>[39m(B[m/var/www/html[36m</tt>[39m(B[m. You[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hcan make your own virtual hosts under /var/www. This is different[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hto previous releases which provides better security out of the box.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;13H[36m</p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;9H[36m</div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H

[1;30r[27;9H[36m<div [31mclass=[32m"section_header"[36m>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<div [31mid=[32m"bugs"[36m></div>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HReporting Problems[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H

[1;30r[27;11H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HPlease use the [36m<tt>[39m(B[mubuntu-bug[36m</tt>[39m(B[m tool to report bugs in the[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[2;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HApache2 package with Ubuntu. However, check <a[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H[31mhref=[32m"https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+source/apache2"[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17H[31mrel=[32m"nofollow"[39m(B[m>existing bug reports[36m</a>[39m(B[m before reporting a new bug.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m</p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;11H[36m<p>[3d[39m(B[m[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17HPlease report bugs specific to modules (such as PHP and others)[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[27;17Hto respective packages, not to the web server itself.[3d[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H

[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
[1;30r[3;1H[?12l[?25h[?25l[3;28r[28;1H
